<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user initially reported a critical issue where the Event Tool frontend could not create orders in the Rental Hub backend due to CORS and 500 errors on the  endpoint.

This has now evolved into a major architectural refactoring. The user provided a detailed technical specification to overhaul the system's concept of clients and payers.

**PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:**
1.  **Decouple Clients from Payers:** A Client (a person/contact) is distinct from a Payer (a legal entity). A single client can have multiple associated payer profiles.
2.  **New Database Schema:**
    *   : Stores contact information (email, phone, name). Email must be the unique identifier.
    *   : Stores legal/billing details for 5 different entity types.
    *   : A linking table between  and .
    *   : Must be linked to a  and an optional .
3.  **Clients Tab in RentalHub:** Create a new Clients tab in the  to manage clients and their associated payer profiles. This is a CRM-lite feature.
4.  **Policy Matrix for Documents:** Legal documents (annexes, acts) can only be generated for an order if a  is assigned. Drafts and quotes can exist without a payer.
5.  **Refactor :** The endpoint must use this new architecture, creating a new  if one doesn't exist (based on email) and linking the new order.
6.  **Update EventTool Checkout:** The checkout process in the EventTool must allow users to select an existing payer profile or specify that details will be provided later, creating an order without a .
